The selloff comes after <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-btc-weekly-fall-elon-musk-tesla-environmental-concerns-2021-5-1030430674\">Tesla reversed its plans to accept bitcoin as payment</a>, with CEO <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/elon-musk-tesla-bitcoin-bad-for-the-environment-carbon-emissions-2021-5\">Elon Musk decrying the environmental toll of its usage</a>. </p><p>Binance, another major crypto exchange, said it was pausing withdrawals. In a <a href=\"https://twitter.com/binance/status/1395002603558391812?s=20\">tweet</a> Wednesday morning, the company said that &#34;$ETH and ERC20 withdrawals are temporarily disabled due to network congestion. Thank you for your patience and apologies for any inconvenience caused.&#34;</p><p>On social media, some users expressed frustration at Coinbase. target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>The boom in retail investing that sent GameStop soaring and shook markets earlier in the year cooled sharply in April, according to research from banks, with analysts suggesting stay-at-home traders found other things to spend their money on as economies reopened.</p><p>US retail trading volumes were down 26% in April compared to a month earlier, according to Piper Sandler analysis. It adds to recent research from <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/retail-trading-stock-market-declined-in-march-despite-stimulus-checks-2021-5-1030410379\">JPMorgan</a> and <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/retail-trading-activity-investors-stock-market-april-goldman-2021-4-1030295308\">Goldman Sachs</a> that has shown a considerable drop in activity among amateur investors.</p><p>&#34;The 2020 stay-at-home orders and business closures have meant many have an abundance of time and money, which bred a huge flurry of retail activity,&#34; Josh Mahony, senior market analyst at trading platform IG, said.</p><p>Yet Mahony said the recent fall in retail trading should come as no surprise. &#34;With <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-guidelines-mask-guidance-list-of-states-relaxing-keeping-mandates-2021-5\">restrictions gradually removed</a> and businesses reopening, the question for the months ahead is just how different the new &#39;normal&#39; looks,&#34; he said.</p><p>Piper Sandler&#39;s research, released to clients earlier in May, found that online investing in futures, cash equity and equity option volumes all decreased month on month in April.</p><p>&#34;Trading activity contracted considerably,&#34; the investment bank&#39;s managing director Richard Repetto and analyst Kyle Robinson wrote.</p><p>Piper Sandler found that April&#39;s equity trading volumes fell to 9.9 billion shares per day in April. That was below 2020&#39;s record average of 10.9 billion shares per day, and sharply down from a peak of 14.7 billion shares per day in the first quarter of 2021.</p><p>JPMorgan analysts led by Nikolaos Panigirtzoglou said in a note on Friday that retail investors seemed to have cut back on options trading in April and early May.</p><p>They added: &#34;Equity baskets containing stocks popular with US retail trading platforms... are conveying a similar message of continued underperformance into May.&#34;</p><p>It marked a change from earlier in the year when the retail-trading frenzy that began in 2020 burst into public view and <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/reddit-day-traders-wallstreetbets-gamestop-gme-rally-upending-stock-market-2021-1-1030009280?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestm=ingest\">caused GameStop stock to skyrocket</a>, hitting short-sellers and unnerving the broader market.</p><p>Analysts have said that the reopening of the US economy and rising vaccination rates could be making day traders feel more comfortable in venturing out and spending their money on other things.</p><p>Goldman Sachs analyst Alexander Blostein said in a note in April the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/stock-market-today-global-shares-inflation-tech-crypto-gold-2021-5-1030445473\">recent mixed performance</a> of stocks could also be putting off amateur investors.</p><p>But the JPMorgan analysts said retail investors still appeared to be buying into exchange-traded funds at a solid rate. And Blostein wrote: &#34;Retail trading still remains significantly above pre-Covid levels, with many structural changes (such as zero commission trading) in place.&#34;</p><div 22:55:45","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","title":"Lex Greensill did have 'some form of contract' while working for David Cameron, senior civil servant tells MPs","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/greensill-had-some-form-of-contract-in-whitehall-mps-told-2021-5","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a51ef0e25d05001880c6e5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"david cameron lex greensill 2\" height=\"649\" width=\"1299\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>David Cameron&#39;s lobbying for Greensill Capital is the subject of multiple official inquiries.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>David Cameron&#39;s former advisor Lex Greensill did, in fact, have a contract while working inside the UK government, the Cabinet Secretary has said.</li>\n<li>Simon Case had previously suggested that Greensill was not a contracted employee.</li>\n<li>However, he now says he has seen appointment letters that suggest &#34;some form of contract&#34; was drawn up.</li>\n<li>Greensill&#39;s role as an unpaid advisor is at the centre of inquiries into lobbying by the former Prime Minister.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Simon Case, the UK government Cabinet Secretary, has told Members of Parliament that the financier Lex Greensill did have some form of government contract while working for former Prime Minister David Cameron, despite previously suggesting no such contract existed.</p><p>Greensill, the Australian billionaire founder of the now-collapsed Greensill Capital, is at the center of a series of inquiries into the lobbying of senior ministers by Cameron on behalf of Greensill Capital.</p><p>One such inquiry is the Boardman Review, investigating the nature and circumstances of the unpaid advisory role held by Greensill in Downing Street and the Cabinet Office in the early 2010s. </p><p>In <a href=\"https://committees.parliament.uk/publications/5896/documents/67255/default/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">a letter to the chair of PACAC</a>, William Wragg MP, published Tuesday, Case sought to clarify comments he and fellow civil servant Darren Tierney, director-general of propriety and ethics at the Cabinet Office, had made to the committee on April 26. </p><p>Case wrote: &#34;Since we gave evidence to the Committee, we have seen signed appointment letters that cover the period from April 2012 to March 2014. As Darren Tierney said to the Committee, the letter of appointment did contain provisions about Mr Greensill&#39;s conflicts of interest and duties on him regarding conduct, propriety and confidentiality.</p><p>&#34;However, my initial assessment of these letters suggests to me that some form of contract was in place whilst he was working for the Cabinet Office.&#34;</p><p>Tierney had previously told the committee that civil servants had not found a contract. He said: &#34;What we have found so far are an appointment letter and then subsequent reappointment letters, which set out some conditions on his appointment-things like the Official Secrets Act, confidentiality, using the Business Appointment Rules when he leaves-but so far we have been unable to identify the contract.&#34;</p><p>A business card for Greensill, obtained by the Labour Party, described Greensill as a &#34;Senior Advisor&#34; in the Prime Minister&#39;s office, including a Downing Street email address and direct landline. Tierney told the committee that Greensill had a pass for the Cabinet Office and Number 10. </p><p>In the committee meeting of April 26, PACAC member David Jones MP asked Tierney if it was possible that Greensill may have acquired &#34;information that would have been of assistance to him in deciding the basis upon which he would offer commercial services to the Government&#34; while working in Downing Street. Tierney described this as a &#34;potential conflict of interest.&#34;</p><p>Jones suggested it looked like a &#34;screaming, glaring conflict of interest&#34;. Tierney replied: &#34;Yes, it does.&#34;</p><p>In his letter, Case told Wragg that as the Boardman Review is ongoing, it was not possible to publish the appointment letters. When asked about the potential to publish the appointment letters or provide them to the committee, Case had previously told the committee that &#34;I cannot think why not, but if there is a reason why not we will let you know.&#34;</p><p>A source on the committee told Insider that the letters have not yet been provided to them.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Wedding arts and crafts and wedding décor rose 150% across April.</p><p>The COVID-19 pandemic forced many couples to re-think their special days. Some brides and grooms have <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/pandemic-wedding-changes-photo-ideas-2021-1\">opted</a> for small, intimate ceremonies, live-streamed vows, or drive-in nuptials. Others canceled or postponed their plans altogether. </p><p>But Gartner Studios - a stationary company and a supplier for Walmart - found that 95% of couples who postponed their 2020 wedding plan to say &#34;I do&#34; in 2021.</p><p>Last year, when the pandemic forced many to rethink social plans, the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/community/large-events/considerations-for-events-gatherings.html\">advised</a> Americans to avoid &#34;large events,&#34; which could include big weddings, although the CDC did not &#34;provide numbers to define small and large events.&#34; </p><p>Researchers from the University of Maryland, University of Western Ontario, and Texas Tech University previously <a href=\"https://journals.sagepub.com/doi/full/10.1177/2378023120980328\">found</a> that there was &#34;a dramatic decrease in year-to-date cumulative marriages in 2020 compared with 2019 &#34; in &#34;settings representing a variety of COVID-19 experiences in the United States.&#34;</p><p>&#34;Year-to-date declines in marriage are unlikely to be due solely to closure of government agencies that administer marriage certification or reporting delays,&#34; the researchers wrote. &#34;Together, these findings suggest that marriage has declined during the COVID-19 outbreak and may continue to do so, at least in the short term.&#34;</p><p>But the emergence of COVID-19 vaccines and the spike in wedding-related spending at Walmart doesn&#39;t mean a season of stress-free marital bliss, either. Until vaccination rates rise considerably, most in-person weddings in the summer of 2021 are advised to require masks as a <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/covid-19-vaccine-does-not-mean-big-wedding-summer-2021-2020-12\">precaution</a>.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a he said.</p><p>Quartz writer John Detrixhe also referenced one of Siemiatkowski&#39;s recent tweets, Klarna had grown so quickly during the pandemic that it no longer fitted inside its New York office, which temporarily shuttered during the lockdown. </p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">-Sebastian Siemiatkowski  (@klarnaseb) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1372298631001354240?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">March 17, 2021</a></blockquote><script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p> </p><p>Klarna has over <a href=\"https://www.klarna.com/international/press/klarna-continues-strong-us-growth-reaching-record-highs-in-customers-retail-partners-and-consumer-app-downloads/\">6,000 retail partners in the US</a> and more than 200,000 globally, including <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/hm-has-a-new-strategy-to-avoid-retails-deadliest-mistake-2019-7\">H&#38;M</a>, Nike, and Peloton. It counts <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/recession-scarred-millennials-opt-for-buy-now-pay-later-shopping-2019-9\">Afterpay and Affirm as its main competitors</a>.</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/explosion-buy-now-pay-later-credit-klarna-regulation-2021-2\" data-e2e-name=\"inline-read-more-link\">Inside the explosion of buy-now, pay-later services like Klarna, as regulators move to legislate a potentially $350 billion industry</a></em></p><p>Until now its focus has been on partnering with larger brands but it&#39;s beginning to shift to smaller businesses too, according to Siemiatkowski. </p><p>The buy-now-pay-later model allows customers to spread the cost of a purchase over four payments. This model has raised concerns among critics and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/explosion-buy-now-pay-later-credit-klarna-regulation-2021-2\">regulators</a> who said it is encouraging young people to spend beyond their means and get into debt. </p><p>But Siemiatkowski said it&#39;s an alternative to a credit card that&#39;s available to all. </p><p>&#34;A lot of people that are using credit cards and are - by the way - living off the means of other people who are revolving... they&#39;re actually forgetting that a lot of people today don&#39;t have access to these products, and other people have taken an active choice not to participate in those products.</p><p>&#34;And that means that they see the benefit of using buy-now-pay-later. href=\"https://www.amazon.com/amazonprime/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=6be517187b8f819025b04b4e7bc8a7d0&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" member-exclusive event. They can get a <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/student/signup/info/?ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1402130811706&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_071520_2020-amazon-prime-day-20&linkId=c5caea10d0f809038d8f9afe2e860804d0f809038d8f9afe2e860804\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">free six-month Prime trial here</a>. Meanwhile, Prime is also discounted ($6/month) for<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/l/16256994011/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=3bb013f271af07fb2b20d9e345ca1cf4&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"> qualifying customers with an EBT or Medicaid card</a>. </p><p>With cheaper competition like <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/walmart-plus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Walmart+</a> entering the scene, you may be wondering which, if any online membership, is better for you. More than 150 million subscribers worldwide evidently think Prime is worth it, but if you&#39;re still on the fence about buying a membership, we&#39;ve rounded up its many benefits below, broken down into four categories: shipping, shopping, entertainment, and services. </p><p>You might even already have Prime but aren&#39;t using it to its full advantage, in which case this list will be a nice refresher for all the benefits you should know about.</p><h2><strong>Amazon Prime Shipping perks</strong></h2><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/amazonprime/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=6be517187b8f819025b04b4e7bc8a7d0&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Free two-day shipping</a>: </strong>The best-known perk, Amazon Prime&#39;s fast delivery service is convenient and applies to just about anything you&#39;ll need from the site. Just look for the Prime logo as you shop. Shopping on Amazon without a subscription will end up costing more and is less convenient than without a Prime membership.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=4&imprToken=9cba751a-bd93-72b7-651&ie=UTF8&node=8729023011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=6682463bb80f1ec1cffe5bfbabc939f9&language=en_USe5bfbabc939f9&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Free same-day shipping</a>:</strong> For select items, Amazon also offers free one-day or even same-day shipping. With Prime Free one-day delivery, there&#39;s no minimum purchase for eligible items to be ordered by the afternoon and get your items by 9 p.m. the next day. For same-day shipping orders, shoppers can order eligible items before noon and get them by 9 p.m. the same day. Orders placed in the afternoon arrive the next day.  <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=4&imprToken=9cba751a-bd93-72b7-651&ie=UTF8&node=8729023011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=6682463bb80f1ec1cffe5bfbabc939f9&language=en_USe5bfbabc939f9&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Check your zip code</a> to see if same-day and one-day options are available near you. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-amazon-day-schedule-deliveries-prime-benefit\">Amazon Day scheduled deliveries</a>: </strong>Amazon Day, available as a delivery option when you check out your shopping cart, allows you to choose any day of the week (except Sunday) to receive all of your orders at one time. Most items that are eligible for Prime&#39;s free two-day shipping and are shipped by Amazon can be ordered with Amazon Day.</p><p>You&#39;re not locked into Amazon Day for all your future orders. Whenever you check out, you can still choose whichever delivery option works best for your situation, whether that&#39;s tomorrow or in a few days on your designated Amazon Day.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=6&imprToken=9cba751a-bd93-72b7-651&ie=UTF8&node=9433645011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=1a22e8b604d0988459b5f6ef3d4ce417&language=en_US5f6ef3d4ce417&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">No-Rush Shipping</a>:</strong> If you can wait a few extra days for your order to arrive, you may be able to earn rewards on future purchases or receive discounts immediately. Rewards are automatically added to your account once your free No-Rush order ships and they are automatically applied to qualifying orders as well. To be clear, these offers have been sparse due to the supply-chain delays and increased demand related to the novel coronavirus pandemic.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?node=17861200011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=ef745c3049e20aa1afb6a018c7b0f8f6&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Key in-home delivery</a>: </strong>Available in select cities and surrounding areas, secure in-home delivery on millions of eligible items is possible with the Key Smart Lock Kit, which can also be used normally to schedule home access for guests, friends, and family. </p><p>On delivery day, you&#39;ll get a notification in the morning with a four-hour delivery window for when the driver will arrive at your home. Right before the driver arrives, you&#39;ll receive an &#34;Arriving Now&#34; notification and can optionally watch the delivery live through the Amazon Key App. </p><p><em>Note: As of 5/26/20, In-Home Delivery is paused until further notice, due to concerns related to the coronavirus. </em></p><p><strong><a href=\"https://amzn.to/2J3xuf3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Amazon Key in-car delivery</a>: </strong>You can also get Amazon packages securely delivered right into your vehicle when it&#39;s parked at a publicly accessible area. As of February 2020, it works with:</p><ul><li>Model year 2015 and newer Buick, Cadillac, Chevrolet, GMC and Volvo vehicles and requires an active connected car service plan, such as OnStar and On Call</li><li>Select Ford 2017 and later model year vehicles equipped with FordPass Connect</li><li>Lincoln 2018 and later model year vehicles equipped with Lincoln Connect</li><li>Select 2018 or newer Honda vehicles equipped with an active HondaLink Remote Package</li><li>2019 or newer Acura RDX equipped with an active AcuraLink Remote Package.</li></ul><p>Similar to in-home delivery, you&#39;ll be able to track the delivery status in real-time. </p><p><em>Note: As of 5/26/20, In-Car Delivery is paused until further notice, due to concerns related to the coronavirus. </em></p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=7&imprToken=9cba751a-bd93-72b7-651&node=18528209011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=5fa107710c2c4e1f0107c0ff0c2ca884&language=en_USf0c2ca884&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Key in-garage delivery</a>: </strong>Yet another option is garage delivery. You&#39;ll need the Amazon Key app and<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B075H7Z5L8/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll1&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=c3ca3a644b6d440aa7d8b9726d0524d5&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"> Smart Garage Kit</a> to get packages delivered directly to your garage, with the same safety precautions in place as the other Key delivery services. Eligibility for garage delivery depends on your garage door type and zip code. </p><h2><strong>Amazon Shopping Benefits</strong></h2><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-prime-day-best-deals\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Prime Day</a>: </strong>You have to be a Prime member to get access to the estimated million deals offered every summer on <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/primeday/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=29e528cf7b8600f2ab8890e4a6d7335e&language=en_USe&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"9b0da3208fd701766c4cfcb63aad1a83\">Amazon Prime Day</a>. Every year, Insider Reviews covers the best Prime Day deals worth shopping. Of course, shoppers don&#39;t need to wait until Prime Day to see discounts. Amazon regularly changes prices on its products, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-deals-on-amazon\">we gather the best deals every day</a>. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/alm/storefront/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=9&imprToken=44ba751e-591c-8cf2-891&almBrandId=QW1hem9uIEZyZXNo&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=2c6ddf5cddf8f42e1ad642df5be1b4d2&language=en_USf5be1b4d2&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Fresh</a>: </strong>Amazon Fresh is now free to use with a Prime membership (it previously cost an extra $15 a month). It lets you skip the long grocery lines by shopping online and picking a delivery window that&#39;s convenient for you. </p><p>As long as your order total is more than $50, you&#39;ll get free delivery. Thanks to the Whole Foods acquisition, organic foods and Whole Foods&#39; 365 brand products are all readily available. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://primenow.amazon.com/ref=HOUD5243213_assoc_sco_aah&tag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20&ascsubtag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20xxxxs-20xxxx\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Prime Now</a>: </strong>Tens of thousands of everyday household items, grocery essentials, and Amazon products can be delivered to you in two hours or less, in select US cities. Delivery windows generally span from 8 a.m. to 10 p.m., though some extend to midnight depending on the city. <a href=\"https://primenow.amazon.com/ref=HOUD5243213_assoc_sco_aah&tag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20&ascsubtag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20xxxxs-20xxxx\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Check your zip code</a> to see if Prime Now is available near you </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/pantry/info/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=10&imprToken=44ba751e-591c-8cf2-891&&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=316f962d427596b401f9bdedf8c499fb&language=en_USdf8c499fb&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Pantry</a>: </strong>Prime Pantry, now free and included with your Prime membership, lets you shop thousands of household essentials, many of which are not available elsewhere on Amazon. Pantry-exclusive coupons save you even more money on these items. Customers receive free shipping on all orders of $35 or more or pay a flat $6 shipping fee for each order they place.</p><p>As a non-Prime member, you can still order through Prime Pantry, but a $6 shipping fee on each order will apply.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&node=16205654011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=70c6b2af86608c64c5dfff335a741756&language=en_US6&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime-Exclusive Discounts</a>: </strong>Only Prime members get deals on certain products and Amazon services, such as free delivery on restaurant orders, savings on dog and pet food, and rotating deals on the latest movies and TV shows through Prime Video. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/goldbox/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=11&imprToken=44ba751e-591c-8cf2-891&gb_f_deals1=dealTypes:LIGHTNING_DEAL,sortOrder:BY_SCORE,dealStates:AVAILABLE%252CWAITLIST%252CWAITLISTFULL%252CEXPIRED%252CSOLDOUT%252CUPCOMING,includedAccessTypes:GIVEAWAY_DEAL&pf_rd_p=56beed47-26cb-401c-95f5-738a157f0f49&pf_rd_s=slot-5&pf_rd_t=701&pf_rd_i=gb_main&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_r=X5X6NKVF5DYHNPJ78VF8&ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=242460f6aca814b3d520c2ca06fcf4b8&language=en_USnkId=242460f6aca814b3d520c2ca06fcf4b8&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Lightning Deals Early Access</a>: </strong>Lightning Deals are called so for a reason - they&#39;re only available for a few hours and can be snatched up quickly before the expiration time. Prime members get an extra 30 minutes to shop deals before they&#39;re officially open. Just look for the &#34;Prime Early Access&#34; label as you shop the page. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-do-you-get-a-lightning-deal-on-amazon-prime-day\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">Learn more about how to get a Lightning Deal on Prime Day here.</a> </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/l/16122413011/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=12&imprToken=44ba751e-591c-8cf2-891&ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=5391e6a743d6d462e2740b3be3e4c7c1&language=en_USbe3e4c7c1&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Wardrobe</a>: </strong>Prime Wardrobe lets you try on and purchase new styles with little hassle. Choose up to eight items across the women&#39;s, men&#39;s, children&#39;s, and baby clothes, shoes, and accessories categories. Then, you&#39;ll have seven days to try them at home and decide what you want to keep. Check out online, then return your unwanted items for free using the resealable box and prepaid shipping label. </p><p>If you want a more personalized experience, you can try Personal Shopper by Prime Wardrobe, which costs $5/month. </p><p><strong>Free standard shipping on <a href=\"https://click.linksynergy.com/deeplink?id=EHFxW6yx8Uo&mid=42352&murl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.shopbop.com%2F%3Fextid%3Daffprg_linkshare_SB-EHFxW6yx8Uo%26cvosrc%3Daffiliate.linkshare.EHFxW6yx8Uo%26clickid%3Dx1B2Md1RjxyJWap08lQuCVrSUklw58zIwx2wSM0%26subid1%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo-wuWtJL0Ee2gj8ERjLDb5VQ%26sharedid%3D42352%3D42352\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Shopbop</a>, <a href=\"https://click.linksynergy.com/deeplink?id=EHFxW6yx8Uo&mid=42353&murl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.eastdane.com%2F%3Fextid%3Daffprg_linkshare_ED-EHFxW6yx8Uo%26cvosrc%3Daffiliate.linkshare.EHFxW6yx8Uo%26clickid%3Dx1B2Md1RjxyJWap08lQuCVrSUklw581Iwx2wSM0%26subid1%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo-FYQ4yQrBHVYxqGQfTR9rDQ%26sharedid%3D42353%3D42353\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">East Dane</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=13&imprToken=44ba751e-591c-8cf2-891&ie=UTF8&node=10772747011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=270598598a84832819953b75e36342de&language=en_US53b75e36342de&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Woot!</a>:</strong> The shipping benefits extend past Amazon.com. Shopbop is an online destination for luxury and designer clothes, shoes, bags, and accessories, East Dane is its menswear counterpart, and Woot! is an Amazon-owned startup that hosts daily flash deals on discounted products. Log in with your Amazon account on these sites to get your shipping perk. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Amazon-Prime-Rewards-Visa-Signature/dp/BT00LN946S/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll1&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=2d0680892f1ee979e757f90154a815b4&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Prime Rewards Visa Signature Card</a>:</strong> the Amazon Prime Rewards Visa Signature Card gets you: </p><ul><li>5% back at Amazon.com and Whole Foods Market </li><li>2% back at restaurants, gas stations, and drugstores </li><li>1% back on all other purchases </li></ul><p>You&#39;ll get a $70 Amazon.com gift card instantly upon approval, and you can redeem your points on Amazon as well as for cash back, gift cards, and travel. </p><h2><strong>Amazon Prime Entertainment</strong></h2><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/video/storefront/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=779e247e65976a325aaa96d4ff12e5d5&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Video</a>: </strong>Stream from a large library of movies and TV shows for free, including Amazon Originals content, and rent the latest releases for low prices. Prime members can also subscribe to over 100 channels (and only pay for the channels they want), including <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/The-Dragon-and-the-Wolf/dp/B06XNSRC1Z/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll1&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=52837aa81a6e1d38daa4ecd513c65873&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">HBO</a>, <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/video/offers/signup/?ie=UTF8&benefitId=showtimeSub&ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1522794598907&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20&linkId=2829d3ad2456b76ad390399ca3f84fd72829d3ad2456b76ad390399ca3f84fd7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Showtime</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/video/offers/signup/?ie=UTF8&benefitId=cbsaacf&ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1524003453609&_encoding=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=pf4&tag=biip_042318_best-amazon-prime-benefits-20&linkId=e46f9d637067ae7268d0022c7d8f86eae46f9d637067ae7268d0022c7d8f86ea\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">CBS All Access</a>. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/music/prime/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=abab0c8df89f6b9b94b8b60a03defefd&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Music</a>:</strong> Prime Music lets you listen to 2 million songs ad-free and on-demand, while Amazon Music Unlimited ($8/month) expands the library to 60 million songs and lets you download them for offline listening on any device. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/kindle-dbs/hz/bookshelf/prime/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=83616c924e9d30a896b4d1fb5e8ddc97&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Reading</a>: </strong>Prime members can choose up to 10 titles at a time from more than 1,000 options. The title will be available to read on any of your devices via the Kindle app and some books also come with Audible narration. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/kindle-dbs/firstreads/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=7ec5edf7efad3977c0ee84a6498bbac9&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Free eBooks</a>: </strong>Get free, early access to one Kindle book from a selection of editors&#39; picks each month or shop the hardcover version for $10 or less. Available genres include contemporary fiction, thriller, science fiction, and memoir. </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=21&imprToken=64ba7521-e1b3-7324-4ce&ie=UTF8&node=15195001011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=6621d01b5e34f75295c383d78b3fdb3b&language=en_US383d78b3fdb3b&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Gaming</a>:</strong> The service, formerly known as Twitch Prime, offers Amazon Prime subscribers a free Twitch channel subscription, free games, free add-on content to games, and a Prime-exclusive chat badge.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ftu/home/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=8dfea71ad77786650f4b6b5febf83346&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><strong>Amazon FreeTime Unlimited</strong></a><strong>: </strong>FreeTime Unlimited offers unlimited access to 13,000 kids&#39; books, movies, TV shows, educational apps, and games. For Prime members, it&#39;s $3/month for a single child or $7 for a family of up to four children. Parents can set controls like time limits and content filters, and personalize the experiences of each child profile. It&#39;s available on Fire Tablets (books, videos, apps), Kindle eReaders (books), and Android phones and tablets (books, videos). </p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/B072J4QS9F/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll1&tag=biip_071520_2020-amazon-prime-day-20&linkId=4ce286e9086dc2f76170e392b8517699&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Prime Book Box</a>: </strong>Prime Book Box is a children&#39;s book subscription that delivers two hardcover books or four board books to kids up to 12 years old. The book selections are popular reader favorites or Amazon Book Editor-approved, so your child can enjoy both classics and new releases.</p><p>Parents can handle preferences like delivery schedule and preview the book options (or let them be a surprise). Each box costs $20/month (your first box is $17/month) and all boxes ship for free. </p><h2><strong>Other Amazon Prime services</strong></h2><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Cloud-Drive-Storage/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ots=1&slotNum=23&imprToken=64ba7521-e1b3-7324-4ce&ie=UTF8&node=13234696011&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=a5afd3895790267b2fce6bd7334914e2&language=en_USe6bd7334914e2&#38;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Amazon Photos</a>: </strong>You can save and share unlimited photos across desktop, mobile, and tablet, and share unlimited photo storage with up to five people. You&#39;ll also get 5 GB for videos and files. Amazon Photos comes pre-installed on Amazon devices, so you can also view your photos from your Fire TV and Echo Show. </p><p>After you turn your photos into prints and other photo gifts through Amazon Prints, you get free standard and expedited shipping.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/myh/households/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&linkCode=ll2&tag=biip_101320_amazon-prime-day-2020-20&linkId=263dc90c5ebc8d4a5cde2201c2a266c1&language=en_USp;language=en_US\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Prime Household</a>: </strong>Two adults and up to four teens and four child profiles may link in a &#39;Household,&#39; allowing everyone in the family to enjoy Prime benefits like free shipping, Prime Video, and Prime Photos and share content like ebooks, audiobooks, apps, and games. </p><p>Another benefit of linking accounts is that adults can approve orders before they&#39;re placed (for teens) and set parental controls on digital content (for kids).</p><h2><strong>How to sign up for Amazon Prime </strong></h2><p>Signing up for an Amazon Prime membership is easy. You can even try Amazon Prime for free for a month. After which, the cost of Amazon Prime depends on what plan you choose:</p><ul><li><strong>Amazon Prime yearly subscription: </strong>If you opt for a full year, you&#39;ll pay an annual fee of $119.</li></ul><ul><li><strong>Amazon Prime monthly subscription: </strong>You can also pay $12.99 a month. </li></ul><ul><li><strong>Prime Student: </strong>If you&#39;re a student with a valid school email address, you can get a six-month trial of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-prime-student\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"5a4c4b02e798af2143eedce000ed8b1d\">Prime Student</a> and then pay 50% less than other Prime users ($6.49/month) after the trial ends.</li></ul><p>For what it&#39;s worth, we highly recommend paying the annual fee. Opting for the steeper, upfront cost will save you about $37 over the monthly price.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" Wynn</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Brooklyn Nets guard James Harden exchanged email with Insider about partnering with Therabody as an athlete ambassador this week after an earlier investment in the company.</li>\n<li>Harden discussed his investment and new role in the tech wellness company, and detailed how Therabody therapies factor into his preparation for the NBA playoffs.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Brooklyn Nets guard James Harden partnered with the tech wellness company <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.theragun.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Therabody</a> this week as an &#34;athlete ambassador,&#34; he announced in part in an email interview with Insider.</p><p>In February, Harden&#39;s 13 Endeavors made an investment in Therabody along with a group of more than 100 names in sports, business, and entertainment. Other investors included Jay-Z, Aaron Rodgers&#39; growth equity fund Rx3 Growth Partners, Kevin Hart&#39;s Hartbeat Ventures, and Kevin Durant and Rich Kleiman&#39;s Thirty Five Ventures.</p><p>In an email exchange with Insider, Harden discussed his investment and new role in the company, and detailed his history of using Therabody&#39;s percussive massage therapy devices in performance recovery, including in his preparation for the 2021 NBA playoffs. </p><p><strong>How did you view Therabody as an investment going into it, in February?</strong></p><p>I had used Therabody products before I became an investor, so I had knowledge of the brand going in, which spurred my investment. I was first introduced to Theragun when I was in Houston. I am lucky enough to have been taught the importance of taking care of my body by world-class trainers and I have had access to incredible technologies, like Theragun, since their inception.</p><p>But I don&#39;t think these products or technologies should be just for the professional athlete, and Therabody is aligned in that. I loved that Theragun rebranded into Therabody last year and expanded the products and services they offer- they are really setting out to break down barriers in the wellness space. Therabody is a brand I truly believe in- like all of my investments. There is so much more to come for them, and I&#39;m excited to be a part of that growth.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a4fce7f27b4c001944541e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"James Harden\" height=\"2624\" width=\"3936\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kenneth Wynn</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>What do you see yourself bringing to this ambassador partnership? What made this the move for you at this time?</strong></p><p>I don&#39;t do anything without putting my all into it. I invested in Therabody because I believe in what they are setting out to do. I&#39;m becoming an ambassador and taking the partnership to the next level because I want more people to understand what their products can do for them. I think specifically within the last year, people are more aware than ever about how they are treating their bodies and what it needs to feel its best- mentally and physically. Everyone deserves self-care, and by partnering with Therabody, I hope I&#39;ll show the world how accessible it is to proactively take care of the mind and body.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a4ff75f27b4c0019445424?format=jpeg\" alt=\"James Harden\" height=\"2624\" width=\"3936\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kenneth Wynn</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>How does the Therabody therapeutic element factor into your preparation for the playoffs here, if it does? What does it involve for you?</strong></p><p>Throughout the years, I&#39;ve learned to be proactive in taking care of my body to feel my best and perform my best during such a long season. Using my Theragun is one of the most important steps in my pregame and postgame routines. Both routines look similar for most games: stretching, listening to music, hydrating, staying focused, and using Theragun. I&#39;ve also started using Therabody&#39;s RecoveryAir pneumatic compression boots, which are amazing at night or on a rest day while playing video games or watching a movie.</p><div href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-cryptocurrencies-china-crypto-crackdown-price-outlook-2021-5-1030445035\">meltdown in cryptocurrencies</a> sent ether tumbling as much as 44% on Wednesday, with the cryptocurrency falling to its lowest levels since March.</p><p>The cryptocurrency, which is a popular medium of exchange for NFTs, is now down roughly 60% from its recent record-high of $4,380. That&#39;s in stark contrast from its parabolic run in late April and early May, in which it more than doubled in a few short weeks.</p><p>Ether&#39;s not the only cryptocurrency that is down big in recent days. Bitcoin has fallen more than 30% since Monday, with much of the weakness stemming from <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/elon-musk-bitcoin-environment-tesla-crypto-bulls-trolling-2021-5-1030435658\">Elon Musk&#39;s weekend tweets</a> and <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-rally-china-bans-banks-crypto-business-btc-2021-5-1030442848\">China reiterating a warning against the speculative asset class.</a></p><p>But bullish investors could see some reprieve as ether tests <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-ether-price-support-levels-downside-technical-analysis-btc-eth-2021-5-1030442270\">a key technical support level,</a> according to technical analyst Katie Stockton of Fairlead Strategies. </p><p>&#34;The magnitude of [ether&#39;s] pullback shows the risk inherent to parabolic rallies, during which support levels are left well behind,&#34; Stockton explained in a Tuesday note. Ether&#39;s support level now stands around $2,038, according to Stockton.</p><p>Ether briefly dipped below that level early Wednesday morning, falling to a low of $1,919. It has since bounced higher above the key support level, and is trading at $2,375 as of publication.</p><p>&#34;We expect the pullback [in ether] to deepen in the near term, after which a consolidation phase may keep hold for a month or two within the context of the long-term uptrend,&#34; Stockton said.</p><p>As traders look to buy the dip in cryptocurrencies, keeping an eye on ether&#39;s key technical support level outlined by Stockton could prove to be a helpful guide.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a break down how ether could overtake bitcoin in market cap - and why the second-largest cryptocurrency will go over at least $25,000 in the short- to medium-term</a></em></p><div coins</a> to a crypto-based COVID-19 relief fund in India, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-05-18/ethereum-inventor-says-he-won-t-get-shiba-inu-tax-write-off\">Bloomberg first reported</a>.</p><p>Buterin said he is taxed as a Singaporean citizen and is not eligible, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-05-18/ethereum-inventor-says-he-won-t-get-shiba-inu-tax-write-off\">Bloomberg first reported</a>. The rules in his country, he said, are &#34;significantly cleaner than in the US or Canada.&#34; </p><p>The 27-year-old on May 13 donated what was, on that day, equivalent to $1 billion. Buterin intended for it to provide India with healthcare and basic-needs items.</p><p>India, currently a global hotspot for the virus, is seeing global record numbers of cases and deaths with an overwhelmed healthcare system unable to cope with shortages in medication, food, and oxygen tanks.</p><p>When news broke of Buterin&#39;s donation, Shiba Inu dropped by around 34% as investors panicked. The meme token the week prior was skyrocketing to almost 1,000%.</p><p>Shiba Inu, founded less than a year ago, took inspiration from dogecoin, a more established meme currency. It even  branded itself as a &#34;<a href=\"https://www.shibatoken.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">dogecoin killer</a>.&#34; Because it&#39;s new, it&#39;s still also very volatile. At one point, the donation of Buterin fell to around $800 million and rose to about $2 billion. </p><p>Shiba Inu was last at $0.000009253 as of 9 a.m. ET Wednesday, according to <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/shiba-inu/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">CoinMarketCap</a>. It is the 33th largest cryptocurrency with a market valuation of over $3.2 billion. At this point. Buterin&#39;s donation is equivalent to $414 million.</p><p>Then, on May 17, Buterin announced that <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/vitalik-buterin-shiba-inu-coin-burn-dogecoin-ethereum-2021-5-1030436920\">he burned 90% of his Shiba Inu holdings</a> - almost half the coin&#39;s circulation. It was his only choice, he said, given that the creators of the meme token sent him trillions of coins without his consent.</p><p>&#34;I don&#39;t *want* to be a locus of power of that kind. Better to just print the coins into the hands of a worthy charity directly (though do talk to them first),&#34; <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/vitalik-buterin-shiba-inu-coin-burn-dogecoin-ethereum-2021-5-1030436920\">he wrote in his note</a>.</p><p>To burn a coin means to send it to an unusable account thereby permanently removing it from circulation.  </p><p>The largest cryptocurrency exchange in India, Binance-owned WazirX exchange, <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/shiba-inu-binance-indian-exchange-dogecoin-ethereum-vitalik-buterin-donation-2021-5-1030431008\">listed Shiba Inu</a> a day after Buterin&#39;s donation. The listing of meme tokens is often seen as a sign of legitimacy in the cryptocurrency community.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/crypto-trading-investing-tips-crypto-tokens-hodling-trader-scott-melker-2021-5\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">&#39;Wolf of All Streets&#39; crypto trader Scott Melker breaks down his strategy for making money using &#39;HODLing&#39; and 100X trade opportunities - and shares 5 under-the-radar tokens he thinks could explode</a></em></p><div to collect product data from multiple sites.</strong></li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Google will partner with e-commerce platform Shopify to let sellers show their products across Google&#39;s platforms, the internet giant announced at its <a href=\"https://events.google.com/io/session/88b34a4e-6170-4f18-a321-4260fb559e60?lng=en\">I/O conference</a> on Tuesday. </p><p>Google did not say exactly how or when Shopify will integrate with Google, but its president of commerce, Bill Ready, said sellers would have their products featured across Google&#39;s 1 billion daily &#34;shopping journeys&#34; taking place on Search, Images, Maps, Lens, and YouTube. </p><p>Ready also said Shopify sellers would link to Google&#39;s &#34;<a href=\"https://blog.google/products/shopping/more-ways-to-shop/\">Shopping Graph</a>&#34;, a new tool that uses machine learning to gather prices, reviews, and product videos from multiple brands and retailers&#39; websites to better inform shoppers. </p><p>The Shopping Graph would connect &#34;people with over 24 billion listings from multiple merchants across the web,&#34; Ready said in a <a href=\"https://blog.google/products/shopping/more-ways-to-shop/\">blog post</a>.  </p><p>In April last year, Google said it would allow merchants to sell their products on its platform for free. Ready said at the time that the change was being introduced to help businesses struggling during the pandemic.</p><p>&#34;For retailers, this change means free exposure to millions of people who come to Google every day for their shopping needs,&#34; Ready said in a <a href=\"https://blog.google/products/shopping/its-now-free-to-sell-on-google/\">blog post</a> at the time. </p><p>Ready said the 2020 change had led to an 80% increase in sellers on Google, and the majority were small to medium-sized businesses. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a (Anna Cooban)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/608a93ff34af8d0018599dc1?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn63@2020_6/2021/05/19/14-56-01-570_e8d43b0794d2d60b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn88@2020_2/2021/05/19/14-56-05-974_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=drkdn3-_b_g:I-OWFPUYPo8:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn96@2020_5/2021/05/19/14-56-03-970_5e7ea430aef24cad.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=drkdn3-_b_g:I-OWFPUYPo8:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn87@2020_5/2021/05/19/14-56-04-229_16896ef7c8f37008.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn71@2020_3/2021/05/19/14-56-33-719_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=drkdn3-_b_g:I-OWFPUYPo8:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn16@2020_2/2021/05/19/14-56-05-838_52775a8d7db2edc3.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/drkdn3-_b_g":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn88@2020_6/2021/05/19/14-56-04-944_d6f6a0c447720263.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1621436145867},{"createdTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","title":"A pediatric infectious disease expert answers 7 common questions about children getting the COVID-19 vaccine","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/questions-children-getting-covid-vaccine-answered-expert-2021-5","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a3ebd8f27b4c0019445147?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Child getting COVID-19 vaccine\" height=\"3279\" width=\"4373\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Charles Muro, age 13, celebrates being inoculated at the Connecticut Convention Center in Hartford, Connecticut, on May 13, 2021.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Joseph Prezioso / AFP via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The FDA expanded emergency use of the Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 vaccine to children aged 12-15 on May 10.</li>\n<li>Expert in pediatric infectious diseases Dr. Debbie-Ann Shirley addressed concerns parents may have.</li>\n<li>She says the vaccine will work, it appears to be safe, and no severe reactions have been reported.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The Food and Drug Administration <a href=\"https://www.fda.gov/news-events/press-announcements/coronavirus-covid-19-update-fda-authorizes-pfizer-biontech-covid-19-vaccine-emergency-use\">expanded emergency use authorization of the Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 vaccine</a> to include adolescents 12 to 15 years of age on May 10, 2021. The Centers for Disease Control and Prevention <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/media/releases/2021/s0512-advisory-committee-signing.html\">followed with recommendations endorsing use</a> in this age group after their advisory group meeting on May 12. The American Academy of Pediatrics <a href=\"https://doi.org/10.1542/peds.2021-052336\">also supports this decision</a>.</p><p><a href=\"https://scholar.google.com/citations?hl=en&user=M6zP_sMAAAAJ&view_op=list_works&gmla=AJsN-F7liTrsfpmCNPxthHwM5Pv-FLx3o9t7WF4FyjfdwmBAG-bKn_5xDQNmYB-HADCzpZ6s21yCrlTQrIvHhXiFG43yFvrU65qXSGvhoJqAFx8K8VaVMeUAFx8K8VaVMeU\">Dr. Debbie-Ann Shirley</a> is an associate professor of pediatrics at the <a href=\"https://uvahealth.com/findadoctor/profile/debbie-ann-shirley\">University of Virginia</a> specializing in pediatric infectious diseases. Here she addresses some of the concerns parents may have about their teen or preteen getting the COVID-19 vaccine.</p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/oracle-svp-outlines-steps-required-return-to-office-safely-2021-1\">Oracle SVP says the gradual return to the workplace will require physical safety and workplace wellbeing. She shares how to make the</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/oracle-svp-outlines-steps-required-return-to-office-safely-2021-1\"> transition.</a></em></p><h2>1. Does the vaccine work in adolescents?</h2><p>Yes, recently released <a href=\"https://www.pfizer.com/news/press-release/press-release-detail/pfizer-biontech-announce-positive-topline-results-pivotal\">data from Pfizer-BioNTech</a> shows that the COVID-19 vaccine seems to work really well in this age group. The COVID-19 vaccine was found to be <a href=\"https://www.pfizer.com/news/press-release/press-release-detail/pfizer-biontech-announce-positive-topline-results-pivotal\">100% efficacious</a> in preventing symptomatic COVID-19 in an ongoing clinical trial of children in the US aged 12 to 15. Adolescents made <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/vaccines/different-vaccines/how-they-work.html\">high levels of antibody</a> in response to the vaccine, and their immune response was just as strong as what has been seen in older teens and young adults 16-25 years of age.</p><h2>2. How do I know whether the vaccine is safe for my child?</h2><p>So far, the COVID-19 vaccine appears to be safe and well tolerated in adolescents. All of the COVID-19 vaccines authorized for use in the US have undergone rigorous study, but we don&#39;t want to assume that children are little adults. This is why it&#39;s so important to study these vaccines just as carefully in children before health authorities could recommend use. Ongoing studies will continue to follow vaccinated children closely and <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/vaccinesafety/ensuringsafety/monitoring/vaers/index.html\">robust safety monitoring</a> will help rapidly identify rare or unexpected concerns if they emerge.</p><h2>3. I thought children were low-risk - do they still need to get the vaccine?</h2><p>Currently, children represent nearly <a href=\"https://services.aap.org/en/pages/2019-novel-coronavirus-covid-19-infections/children-and-covid-19-state-level-data-report/\">25% of all new reported weekly COVID-19 cases</a> in the US. While serious illness from COVID-19 is rare in children, it does occur - thousands of children have been hospitalized and <a href=\"https://covid.cdc.gov/covid-data-tracker/#demographics\">at least 351 children</a> have died from COVID-19 in the US. Some children who get seriously ill from COVID-19 may have underlying health conditions, but not all do. Vaccination will help protect children from developing serious illness.</p><p>Additionally, since adolescents can transmit COVID-19 to others, vaccinating children may prove to be an important part of safely getting back to normal activities of life, including attending school in person, participating in team sports, and spending time with friends. <a href=\"http://dx.doi.org/10.15585/mmwr.mm7011a1\">A large survey of school-aged children</a> showed that children in full or partial virtual school reported lower levels of physical activity, less in-person time socializing with friends, and worse mental or emotional health compared with those receiving full in-person schooling. Children are experiencing unprecedented increases in indirect adverse health and educational consequences related to the pandemic, and we need to find ways to help them get quickly and safely back to normal life. Vaccination is one of them.</p><h2>4. What side effects might I expect for my child?</h2><p>Nonsevere side effects may be experienced following vaccination. The <a href=\"https://www.fda.gov/media/144413/download\">most commonly reported side effects</a> have been pain and swelling at the injection site. Other common side effects include tiredness and headache. Similar to young adults, some adolescents have experienced fever, chills, muscle aches, and joint pain, which may be more common after the second dose. These effects are short-lived, however, and most resolve within one to two days.</p><p>Some adolescents <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/vaccinesafety/concerns/fainting.html\">may faint</a> when receiving an injection. If this is a concern for your child, let your vaccine administration site know ahead of time - your child can be given the vaccine while they&#39;re seated or lying down to avoid injuries from falling.</p><h2>5. Have there been any severe reactions among children?</h2><p><a href=\"https://www.pfizer.com/news/press-release/press-release-detail/pfizer-biontech-announce-positive-topline-results-pivotal\">No serious adverse events</a> related to vaccination were reported in the Pfizer-BioNTech clinical trial. Serious allergic reactions have rarely been reported in older people. Anyone with a known severe or immediate allergy to the vaccine or any component of the vaccine should not get the vaccine. If your child has a history of any severe allergic reactions or any type of immediate allergic reaction to a vaccine or injectable therapy, let the vaccine site administrator know so that your child can be monitored for at <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/vaccines/safety/allergic-reaction.html?s_cid=10485:who%20should%20not%20take%20the%20covid%20vaccine:sem.ga:p:RG:GM:gen:PTN:FY21\">least 30 minutes after getting the vaccine</a>.</p><p>Parents should talk to a trusted health care provider or allergist if they have specific questions about the possibility of an allergic reaction in their child.</p><h2>6. When will a COVID-19 vaccine be authorized for children younger than 12 years?</h2><p>COVID-19 vaccine makers have begun or are planning to begin testing COVID-19 vaccines in younger children. As more information becomes available, the authorized age recommendations may change. Children ages two-11 years old could potentially be eligible as early as the end of this year.</p><h2>7. If I&#39;ve been vaccinated but my child hasn&#39;t, could I still give the virus to them?</h2><p>The COVID-19 vaccines <a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/vaccines/facts.html\">do not contain live COVID-19 virus</a>, so they cannot cause COVID-19. Rather, getting vaccinated will help protect both you and your children from COVID-19. Studies have shown that vaccinated pregnant and lactating mothers can pass protective immunity on to their young infants <a href=\"https://doi.org/10.1016/j.ajog.2021.03.023\">across the placenta and in breast milk</a> - one more benefit of vaccination.</p><p>Though researchers are still learning how well the vaccine can help prevent spread, vaccination is still an important way to limit infecting people who are not yet eligible for the vaccine, like younger children.<!-- Below is The Conversation's page counter tag. pediatrics, <a href=\"https://theconversation.com/institutions/university-of-virginia-752\">University of Virginia</a></em></p><div class=\"insider-raw-embed\"><figure>\n\t<img 22:55:45","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","title":"The hackers who shut down Colonial Pipeline brought in over $90 million in bitcoin ransoms while in operation","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/colonial-pipeline-hack-ransom-cryptocurrency-darkside-2021-5","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a408f91b5cea0019c458b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"colonial pipeline darkside hacking ransomware\" height=\"4017\" width=\"5356\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A sign is seen at Colonial Pipeline Baltimore Delivery in Baltimore, Maryland on May 10, 2021. - The US government declared a regional emergency Son May 9, 2021 as the largest fuel pipeline system in the United States remained largely shut down, two days after a major ransomware attack was detected. The Colonial Pipeline Company ships gasoline and jet fuel from the Gulf Coast of Texas to the populous East Coast through 5,500 miles (8,850 kilometers) of pipeline, serving 50 million consumers. The company said it was the victim of a cybersecurity attack involving ransomware -- attacks that encrypt computer systems and seek to extract payments from operators.\n<p class=\"copyright\">JIM WATSON/AFP via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>DarkSide brought in over $90 million through ransomware cyberattacks, according to new research.</li>\n<li>The group emptied its Bitcoin wallets on May 13 after national scrutiny. </li>\n<li>Elliptic tracked payments to the group&#39;s Bitcoin wallets to make the $90 million estimate. </li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>DarkSide Ransomware, the group that mounted a cyberattack on the Colonial Pipeline earlier this month, has brought in over $90 million in bitcoin ransom payments over the course of its operation, according to <a href=\"https://www.elliptic.co/blog/darkside-ransomware-has-netted-over-90-million-in-bitcoin\">new research from blockchain-analytics firm Elliptic</a>.</p><p>Elliptic found that there were 47 bitcoin wallets - that is, digital cryptocurrency accounts belonging to distinct entities - that paid Bitcoin ransoms to the group of hackers. The total amount of the ransoms, paid in untraceable cryptocurrencies, was more than $90 million. The group became active in October 2020 and scaled up its operations in 2021. </p><p>DarkSide said it planned to disband following pressure from the US government and law enforcement officials, <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/web-site-of-darkside-hacking-group-linked-to-colonial-pipeline-attack-is-down-11621001688\">according to The Wall Street Journal</a>,</p><p>DarkSide <a href=\"https://twitter.com/darktracer_int/status/1391735232991092738?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1391735232991092738%7Ctwgr%5E%7Ctwcon%5Es1_&ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.businessinsider.com%2Fcolonial-pipeline-hack-darkside-says-will-introduce-moderation-future-targets-2021-521-5\">released a statement on Twitter</a> shortly after the cyberattack saying that it is an &#34;apolitical&#34; group, and &#34;our goal is to make money and not creating problems for society.&#34; </p><p>The group&#39;s bitcoin wallet was emptied on May 13, according to Elliptic, but not before the Colonial Pipeline <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/hackers-get-5-million-after-causing-major-gas-shortage-2021-5\">transferred hackers nearly $5 million in cryptocurrency</a>. </p><p>After the Colonial Pipeline sent the payment, DarkSide provided the company with a decryption tool to help get its systems online after the attack. However, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-05-13/colonial-pipeline-paid-hackers-nearly-5-million-in-ransom?srnd=premium&sref=BWbpWjRmWjRm\">Bloomberg reported</a> that the tool worked too slowly and the company kept using existing backups to bring things back online.</p><p>The system was closed for six days as a result of the DarkSide attack. The pipeline supplies almost half of the fuel used on the East Coast. The company <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/etf/fuel-crisis-eases-as-colonial-pipeline-returns-to-normal-after-ransomware-attack-1030432719\">announced</a> on Saturday, May 16 that the pipeline was back to full operations, although there were outages on Tuesday. <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/colonial-pipeline-scheduling-system-for-nations-largest-pipeline-shut-down-2021-5\">The cause of the network issues</a> on Tuesday was not immediately apparent. </p><p>Elliptic reported that affiliates of DarkSide split the funds from ransom payments with developers who worked on the actual malware. &#34;The DarkSide developer has received bitcoins worth $15.5 million (17%), with the remaining $74.7 million (83%) going to the various affiliates,&#34; Elliptic reported, with the share for developers starting out at 25% and decreasing to 5% if the ransom amounts to over $5 million. </p><p>Ransomware attacks are on the rise in the US, with Temple University data cited by the Washington Post showing a record high of almost 400 attacks in 2020. <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2021/05/12/ransomware-attack/\">The Washington Post reported</a> that experts are concerned about the trend as hackers target cities, hospitals, and critical infrastructure this year. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a (Annabelle Williams)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/60a408f91b5cea0019c458b2?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn96@2020_1/2021/05/19/14-56-03-136_8f290b955525d586.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn88@2020_2/2021/05/19/14-56-05-974_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=05fLP74Cc-8:oSdPzj67P_w:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn92@2020_6/2021/05/19/14-56-02-113_5ce0ef14a42e8e6d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=05fLP74Cc-8:oSdPzj67P_w:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn44@2020_1/2021/05/19/14-56-03-452_56bccf93fa32db40.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn71@2020_3/2021/05/19/14-56-33-719_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=05fLP74Cc-8:oSdPzj67P_w:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn60@2020_6/2021/05/19/14-56-07-133_a8744e86524b14f7.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/05fLP74Cc-8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn31@2020_2/2021/05/19/14-56-03-950_584af5999d4de491.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1621436145871},{"createdTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:55:45","title":"2 factors not included in the CDC guidelines can help you decide when it's really safe to go maskless","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-decide-when-safe-to-remove-mask-cdc-2021-5","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60a3d1c81b5cea0019c45764?format=jpeg\" alt=\"mask hair salon\" height=\"1867\" width=\"2800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Gerri Gold, 81, holds her mask in place as Kathy Ly, a hair stylist at The Headline Salon in Woodland Hills, California, trims around her ear on May 13, 2021.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Mel Melcon/Los Angeles Times/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-says-fully-vaccinated-people-can-drop-masks-most-places-2021-5\">Fully vaccinated people can ditch their masks</a> at any indoor or outdoor gathering, per the CDC.</li>\n<li>But public-health experts caution that this advice <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-guidelines-no-masks-vaccinated-people-expert-opinion-2021-5\">might not apply to all communities</a>.</li>\n<li>If cases in your local area start to rise or few people have been vaccinated there, consider a mask.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>When the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention announced last week that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-says-fully-vaccinated-people-can-drop-masks-most-places-2021-5\">fully vaccinated people could ditch their masks</a>, many Americans - and some public-health experts - wondered whether the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-guidelines-no-masks-vaccinated-people-expert-opinion-2021-5\">recommendations were too broad</a>.</p><p>&#34;We&#39;re missing a critical step, and that step is fully vaccinated people around other fully vaccinated people in large or small groups,&#34; Leana Wen, the former health commissioner of Baltimore, told Insider. &#34;That should be safe, but now we&#39;re going from &#39;you can only dine indoors with a few people&#39; to &#39;everybody can take off their masks because we&#39;re not checking their vaccination status.&#39;&#34;</p><p>The CDC&#39;s recent guidance says that fully vaccinated Americans can take off their masks indoors and outdoors at gatherings of any size - even with unvaccinated people present. The exceptions to that rule include healthcare settings, homeless shelters, public transportation, and airports. Private companies such as stores and airlines are also be free to enforce mask rules as they see fit.</p><p>But for people who want a more tailored way to gauge their personal risk, experts highlight two circumstances in which masks are still a good idea for vaccinated people. The first is if new daily cases start to rise at all in your local community. The second is a low level of vaccination in your area - one significantly below the current national average of 37%.</p><p>But even in the absence of these red flags, experts noted, the CDC is not mandating that anyone to go maskless. </p><p>&#34;It doesn&#39;t mean that you have to take your mask off,&#34; Anne Rimoin, an epidemiology professor at the University of California, Los Angeles, told Insider. &#34;It means that you <em>can</em> take your mask off.&#34;</p><p>She added: &#34;If you are still feeling vulnerable, if you&#39;re somebody who has a compromised immune system, if you are in an area when you&#39;re still higher transmission, then the conservative thing to do would be to continue to wear a mask in situations where you&#39;re going to be around people where you don&#39;t know what their vaccination status is.&#34;</p><h2>Any increase in cases could be a reason to mask up</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606309ef67187800184ad3c5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"coronavirus testing\" height=\"1105\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A nurse administers a COVID-19 test at a site in Suffolk County, New York, on December 18, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/detail/news-photo/nurse-practitioner-deborah-beauplan-administers-a-covid-19-news-photo/1296362947?adppopup=true\" target=\"_blank\">John Paraskevas/Newsday via Getty Images</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The more real-life data researchers get about the US&#39;s authorized vaccines, the more the shots seem to work <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-vaccines-exceeding-expectations-real-world-data-2021-5\">well against variants</a> and reduce transmission. So Rimoin said the new CDC guidelines simply underscore &#34;how confident we are in these vaccines and the ability of these vaccines to really protect people.&#34;</p><p>President Joe Biden <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/us-will-send-vaccine-supply-overseas-after-who-criticism-2021-5\">announced on Monday</a> that US coronavirus cases are declining in all 50 states for the first time since the pandemic started. It&#39;s another indicator that vaccines are stopping the virus from spreading. </p><p>But it also means that any increase in cases in your local area should be concerning at this point, according to Lisa Lee, an epidemiologist at Virginia Tech.</p><p>&#34;If we get an uptick, we&#39;re going to have to consider what is happening because we have a lot of people vaccinated and we should not be seeing more infections,&#34; Lee told Insider. &#34;We should continue to see less.&#34;</p><p>If cases start rising in your community, she said, that&#39;s a good reason to consider putting a mask on - especially when indoors around other people.</p><p>&#34;In a place like rural Colorado that happens to be a hotspot, people have to think carefully,&#34; Lee said. &#34;Even vaccinated folks need to really be careful and think about whether that&#39;s a risk they&#39;re willing to take.&#34;</p><h2>Is your area&#39;s vaccination rate below the national average?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6025b58ab3c2a800183cc7c1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Disneyland vaccines\" height=\"1992\" width=\"3000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Disneyland COVID-19 vaccination site in Anaheim, California.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Mario Tama/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Around 37% of the total US population is fully vaccinated so far. Vaccinated people living in communities that are significantly below that threshold might consider keeping their masks on for now, Lee said.</p><p>&#34;When we say the United States has nearly 50% of people fully vaccinated now, that&#39;s great, but that doesn&#39;t mean anything for a particular place,&#34; Lee said, referring to the roughly 47% of US adults who are fully vaccinated. &#34;We really do need to think carefully about our own situation and our own community.&#34;</p><p>It&#39;s safer to remove your mask, for instance, in McKinley County, New Mexico, or Essex County, New York, where more than half the population is fully vaccinated, than in Warren County, Virginia, or Hancock County, Georgia, where just 3% of residents are fully vaccinated.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/602570f3b3c2a800183cc5c5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"woman face mask\" height=\"2688\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A woman adjusts her face mask.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Those who want to exercise maximum caution could wait to remove their masks until at least 75% of their community is vaccinated, Lee added. That&#39;s likely the threshold at which an area has reached herd immunity - the point beyond which the virus can&#39;t easily pass from person to person.</p><p>Reaching herd immunity would also make it far less likely that the US would suddenly see a new, more contagious or deadly variant emerge. (The virus can&#39;t mutate if it isn&#39;t spreading.)</p><p>&#34;We want to get out of this cycle of chasing the variants with vaccines,&#34; Lee said. &#34;A way we&#39;re going to get out ahead of it is by ensuring that we get 75% to 85% of the population vaccinated. So we&#39;ve got to work on that. We cannot give up.&#34;</p><p>Until then, though, the threat of new variants means there&#39;s always a chance the CDC might need to reinstate mask guidelines.</p><p>&#34;We have to watch for variants that might evade the efficacy of the vaccine,&#34; Lee said. &#34;If we see those, we&#39;re going to have to be flexible enough to agree that, OK, maybe it is time for a few weeks or months of masks again.&#34;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-decide-when-safe-to-remove-mask-cdc-2021-5'>Business Insider</a></div><div
